defined_text = {
	name = Get_GNG_Econ_Year_Short
	text = {
		trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { year = date_no }
			divide_temp_variable = { year = 12 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { year = 0.49 }
			round_temp_variable = year
			add_to_temp_variable = { year = 60 }
		}
		localization_key = "'[?year]"
	}
}
